msg:It is not worthy of the standard of a five-star hotel. There is no hot water. I called and called twice, but no one came. The operator's explanation was that I haven't gone to work yet. At eight in the morning, shouldn't it be a 24-hour after-sales service? According to this argument, you can only wait or take a cold shower if there is no hot water in the middle of the night? Service awareness is really poor. . . Half an hour later, the hot water came, and I found that the shower gel was not replaced in time. It was empty. I called again. This time the response was faster. When I got to the door, I raised my hand and asked the guests to pick it up at the door, speechless. . .
The room together is even weirder, with two bottles of shower gel and no shampoo. . .
The carpet was not cleaned, the hair rope from the previous family was still on the carpet. . . It is estimated that the low-level service encountered in the hotel has been encountered at one time, so why do you want to open a Wanda Realm, which is more expensive than the Wanda on the side. . .
